自然语言处理

[NLP-0] MM-Vet v2: A Challenging Benchmark to Evaluate Large Multimodal Models for Integrated Capabilities
[NLP-0] MM-Vet v2：评估大型多模式模型综合能力的挑战基准

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00765
作者: Weihao Yu,Zhengyuan Yang,Linfeng Ren,Linjie Li,Jianfeng Wang,Kevin Lin,Chung-Ching Lin,Zicheng Liu,Lijuan Wang,Xinchao Wang
关键词-EN: evaluating integrated capabilities, open-ended vision-language questions, vision-language questions targeting, integrated capabilities, open-ended vision-language
关键词-ZN: 评估综合能力、开放式视觉语言问题、瞄准视觉语言问题、综合能力、开放式视觉语言
类目: Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition (cs.CV); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注: Extension of MM-Vet: arXiv:2308.02490

点击查看摘要

Abstract:MM-Vet, with open-ended vision-language questions targeting at evaluating integrated capabilities, has become one of the most popular benchmarks for large multimodal model evaluation. MM-Vet assesses six core vision-language (VL) capabilities: recognition, knowledge, spatial awareness, language generation, OCR, and math. However, its question format is restricted to single image-text pairs, lacking the interleaved image and text sequences prevalent in real-world scenarios. To address this limitation, we introduce MM-Vet v2, which includes a new VL capability called “image-text sequence understanding”, evaluating models’ ability to process VL sequences. Furthermore, we maintain the high quality of evaluation samples while further expanding the evaluation set size. Using MM-Vet v2 to benchmark large multimodal models, we found that Claude 3.5 Sonnet is the best model with a score of 71.8, slightly outperforming GPT-4o which scored 71.0. Among open-weight models, InternVL2-Llama3-76B leads with a score of 68.4.
摘要：MM-VET具有开放式的视觉语言问题，旨在评估综合能力，已成为大型多通道模型评估的最受欢迎的基准之一。MM-Vet评估了六种核心视觉语言(VL)能力：识别、知识、空间意识、语言生成、OCR和数学。然而，它的问题格式仅限于单个图文对，缺乏现实世界场景中普遍存在的交错图文序列。为了解决这一局限性，我们引入了MM-Vet v2，它包括一种新的VL能力，称为“图像-文本序列理解”，评估模型处理VL序列的能力。此外，我们在保持高质量的评价样本的同时，进一步扩大了评价集的规模。使用MM-Vet v2对大型多通道模型进行基准测试，我们发现克劳德3.5十四行诗是最好的模型，得分为71.8，略高于GPT-40的得分71.0。在公开重量模型中，InternVL2-Llama3-76B以68.4分领先。

[NLP-1] Agent Gen: Enhancing Planning Abilities for Large Language Model based Agent via Environment and Task Generation
[NLP-1] AgentGen：通过环境和任务生成增强基于大型语言模型的代理的规划能力

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00764
作者: Mengkang Hu,Pu Zhao,Can Xu,Qingfeng Sun,Jianguang Lou,Qingwei Lin,Ping Luo,Saravan Rajmohan,Dongmei Zhang
关键词-EN: Large Language Model, Large Language, Language Model, garnered significant attention, increasingly popular
关键词-ZN: 大语言模型、大语言、语言模型受到广泛关注，日益流行
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Machine Learning (cs.LG)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Large Language Model (LLM) based agents have garnered significant attention and are becoming increasingly popular. Furthermore, planning ability is a crucial component of an LLM-based agent, involving interaction with the environment and executing actions to complete a planning task, which generally entails achieving a desired goal from an initial state. This paper investigates enhancing the planning abilities of LLMs through instruction tuning, referred to as agent training. Recent studies have demonstrated that utilizing expert-level trajectory for instruction-tuning LLMs effectively enhances their planning capabilities. However, existing work primarily focuses on synthesizing trajectories from manually designed planning tasks and environments. The labor-intensive nature of creating these environments and tasks impedes the generation of sufficiently varied and extensive trajectories. To address this limitation, this paper explores the automated synthesis of diverse environments and a gradual range of planning tasks, from easy to difficult. We introduce a framework, AgentGen, that leverages LLMs first to generate environments and subsequently generate planning tasks conditioned on these environments. Specifically, to improve environmental diversity, we propose using an inspiration corpus composed of various domain-specific text segments as the context for synthesizing environments. Moreover, to increase the difficulty diversity of generated planning tasks, we propose a bidirectional evolution method, Bi-Evol, that evolves planning tasks from easier and harder directions to synthesize a task set with a smoother difficulty curve. The evaluation results derived from AgentBoard show that AgentGen greatly improves LLMs’ planning ability, e.g., the AgentGen instruction-tuned Llama-3 8B surpasses GPT-3.5 in overall performance. Moreover, in certain tasks, it even outperforms GPT-4.
摘要：基于大语言模型(LLM)的代理已经引起了人们的广泛关注，并变得越来越流行。此外，规划能力是基于LLM的代理的关键组成部分，涉及与环境的交互和执行完成规划任务的操作，这通常需要从初始状态实现期望的目标。本文研究了通过指令调优来提高LLMS的规划能力，称为代理培训。最近的研究表明，利用专家级轨迹进行指令调整可以有效地增强LLM的规划能力。然而，现有的工作主要集中在从人工设计的规划任务和环境中综合轨迹。创造这些环境和任务的劳动密集型性质阻碍了足够多样和广泛的轨迹的产生。为了解决这一限制，本文探索了不同环境的自动合成和从容易到困难的逐步范围的规划任务。我们引入了一个框架AgentGen，它首先利用LLMS来生成环境，然后生成以这些环境为条件的计划任务。具体地说，为了提高环境多样性，我们建议使用由各种特定领域的文本片段组成的灵感语料库作为合成环境的上下文。此外，为了增加生成的计划任务的难度多样性，我们提出了一种双向进化方法，该方法将计划任务从较容易和较难的方向进化为具有更平滑难度曲线的任务集。来自AgentBoard的评估结果表明，AgentGen极大地提高了LLMS的规划能力，例如，AgentGen指令调优的LLAMA-38B在整体性能上超过了GPT-3.5。此外，在某些任务中，它的表现甚至超过了GPT-4。

[NLP-2] amper-Resistant Safeguards for Open-Weight LLMs WWW
[NLP-2] 空重量LLM的耐电流保障措施

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00761
作者: Rishub Tamirisa,Bhrugu Bharathi,Long Phan,Andy Zhou,Alice Gatti,Tarun Suresh,Maxwell Lin,Justin Wang,Rowan Wang,Ron Arel,Andy Zou,Dawn Song,Bo Li,Dan Hendrycks,Mantas Mazeika
关键词-EN: raised widespread concerns, Rapid advances, large language models, large language, raised widespread
关键词-ZN: 引发广泛关注，快速进步，大型语言模型，大型语言，引发广泛关注
类目: Machine Learning (cs.LG); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注: Website: this https URL

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Rapid advances in the capabilities of large language models (LLMs) have raised widespread concerns regarding their potential for malicious use. Open-weight LLMs present unique challenges, as existing safeguards lack robustness to tampering attacks that modify model weights. For example, recent works have demonstrated that refusal and unlearning safeguards can be trivially removed with a few steps of fine-tuning. These vulnerabilities necessitate new approaches for enabling the safe release of open-weight LLMs. We develop a method, called TAR, for building tamper-resistant safeguards into open-weight LLMs such that adversaries cannot remove the safeguards even after thousands of steps of fine-tuning. In extensive evaluations and red teaming analyses, we find that our method greatly improves tamper-resistance while preserving benign capabilities. Our results demonstrate that tamper-resistance is a tractable problem, opening up a promising new avenue to improve the safety and security of open-weight LLMs.
摘要：大型语言模型(LLM)能力的快速发展引起了人们对其潜在恶意使用的广泛关注。开放重量LLM提出了独特的挑战，因为现有的保障措施缺乏对篡改模型权重的篡改攻击的稳健性。例如，最近的研究表明，通过几个步骤的微调，就可以很容易地消除拒绝和遗忘的保障措施。这些漏洞需要新的方法来实现安全释放未加重量的低密度脂蛋白。我们开发了一种名为TAR的方法，用于在开放重量的LLM中构建防篡改保护措施，以便对手即使在数千个步骤的微调之后也无法移除这些保护措施。在广泛的评估和红团队分析中，我们发现我们的方法在保持良性性能的同时大大提高了防篡改能力。我们的结果表明，防篡改是一个容易解决的问题，为提高开重LLMS的安全性开辟了一条很有前途的新途径。

[NLP-3] CERT-ED: Certifiably Robust Text Classification for Edit Distance
[NLP-3] CERT-ED：针对编辑距离的可认证鲁棒文本分类

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00728
作者: Zhuoqun Huang,Neil G Marchant,Olga Ohrimenko,Benjamin I. P. Rubinstein
关键词-EN: daily life, growing integration, systems to inference-time, randomized smoothing, edit distance operations
关键词-ZN: 日常生活、不断增强的集成度、系统到推理时间、随机平滑、编辑距离操作
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Cryptography and Security (cs.CR); Machine Learning (cs.LG)
备注: 22 pages, 3 figures, 12 tables. Include 11 pages of appendices

点击查看摘要

Abstract:With the growing integration of AI in daily life, ensuring the robustness of systems to inference-time attacks is crucial. Among the approaches for certifying robustness to such adversarial examples, randomized smoothing has emerged as highly promising due to its nature as a wrapper around arbitrary black-box models. Previous work on randomized smoothing in natural language processing has primarily focused on specific subsets of edit distance operations, such as synonym substitution or word insertion, without exploring the certification of all edit operations. In this paper, we adapt Randomized Deletion (Huang et al., 2023) and propose, CERTified Edit Distance defense (CERT-ED) for natural language classification. Through comprehensive experiments, we demonstrate that CERT-ED outperforms the existing Hamming distance method RanMASK (Zeng et al., 2023) in 4 out of 5 datasets in terms of both accuracy and the cardinality of the certificate. By covering various threat models, including 5 direct and 5 transfer attacks, our method improves empirical robustness in 38 out of 50 settings.
摘要：随着人工智能在日常生活中的日益融合，确保系统对推理时攻击的健壮性至关重要。在证明对这种对抗性例子的稳健性的方法中，随机平滑因其作为任意黑盒模型的包装器的性质而变得非常有前途。以前关于自然语言处理中的随机化平滑的工作主要集中在编辑距离操作的特定子集上，例如同义词替换或单词插入，而没有探索所有编辑操作的认证。在本文中，我们采用了随机化删除(Huang等人，2023)，并提出了用于自然语言分类的认证编辑距离防御(CERT-ED)。通过综合实验，我们证明了CERT-ED在5个数据集中的4个上优于现有的Hamming距离方法RanMASK(Zeng等人，2023)，无论是在准确率上还是在证书的基数上。通过覆盖各种威胁模型，包括5个直接攻击和5个转移攻击，我们的方法在50种设置中的38种情况下提高了经验稳健性。

[NLP-4] Improving Retrieval-Augmented Generation in Medicine with Iterative Follow-up Questions
[NLP-4] 通过迭代后续问题改进医学中的检索增强生成

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00727
作者: Guangzhi Xiong,Qiao Jin,Xiao Wang,Minjia Zhang,Zhiyong Lu,Aidong Zhang
关键词-EN: demonstrated great potential, large language models, follow-up queries, emergent abilities, abilities of large
关键词-ZN: 展示了巨大的潜力、大型语言模型、后续查询、紧急能力、大型能力
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:The emergent abilities of large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated great potential in solving medical questions. They can possess considerable medical knowledge, but may still hallucinate and are inflexible in the knowledge updates. While Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has been proposed to enhance the medical question-answering capabilities of LLMs with external knowledge bases, it may still fail in complex cases where multiple rounds of information-seeking are required. To address such an issue, we propose iterative RAG for medicine (i-MedRAG), where LLMs can iteratively ask follow-up queries based on previous information-seeking attempts. In each iteration of i-MedRAG, the follow-up queries will be answered by a vanilla RAG system and they will be further used to guide the query generation in the next iteration. Our experiments show the improved performance of various LLMs brought by i-MedRAG compared with vanilla RAG on complex questions from clinical vignettes in the United States Medical Licensing Examination (USMLE), as well as various knowledge tests in the Massive Multitask Language Understanding (MMLU) dataset. Notably, our zero-shot i-MedRAG outperforms all existing prompt engineering and fine-tuning methods on GPT-3.5, achieving an accuracy of 69.68% on the MedQA dataset. In addition, we characterize the scaling properties of i-MedRAG with different iterations of follow-up queries and different numbers of queries per iteration. Our case studies show that i-MedRAG can flexibly ask follow-up queries to form reasoning chains, providing an in-depth analysis of medical questions. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first-of-its-kind study on incorporating follow-up queries into medical RAG.
摘要：大型语言模型的涌现能力在解决医学问题方面显示出巨大的潜力。他们可以拥有相当多的医学知识，但可能仍然会产生幻觉，在知识更新方面缺乏灵活性。虽然检索-增强生成(RAG)已被提出利用外部知识库来增强LLMS的医疗问答能力，但它在需要多轮信息搜索的复杂情况下仍然可能失败。为了解决这一问题，我们提出了医学迭代RAG(I-MedRAG)，其中LLMS可以基于先前的信息搜索尝试迭代地询问后续查询。在I-MedRAG的每一次迭代中，后续查询将由一个普通RAG系统回答，并将进一步用于指导下一次迭代的查询生成。我们的实验表明，与普通RAG相比，I-MedRAG在美国执业资格考试(USMLE)中临床片段中的复杂问题上的性能有所提高，并且在海量多任务语言理解(MMLU)数据集上进行了各种知识测试。值得注意的是，我们的零激发I-MedRAG在GPT-3.5上的表现优于所有现有的即时工程和微调方法，在MedQA数据集上的准确率达到69.68%。此外，我们还刻画了I-MedRAG在不同的后续查询迭代次数和不同的每次迭代查询数下的伸缩性。我们的案例研究表明，I-MedRAG可以灵活地提出后续查询，形成推理链，提供对医学问题的深入分析。据我们所知，这是第一次将后续询问纳入医疗抹布的研究。

[NLP-5] Improving Text Embeddings for Smaller Language Models Using Contrastive Fine-tuning
[NLP-5] 使用对比微调改进较小语言模型的文本嵌入

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00690
作者: Trapoom Ukarapol,Zhicheng Lee,Amy Xin
关键词-EN: Large Language Models, resource-intensive nature makes, natural language understanding, Models show remarkable, Large Language
关键词-ZN: 大型语言模型、资源密集型自然制造、自然语言理解、模型表现出色、大型语言
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注: Code: this https URL , Huggingface: this https URL

点击查看摘要

Abstract:While Large Language Models show remarkable performance in natural language understanding, their resource-intensive nature makes them less accessible. In contrast, smaller language models such as MiniCPM offer more sustainable scalability, but often underperform without specialized optimization. In this paper, we explore the enhancement of smaller language models through the improvement of their text embeddings. We select three language models, MiniCPM, Phi-2, and Gemma, to conduct contrastive fine-tuning on the NLI dataset. Our results demonstrate that this fine-tuning method enhances the quality of text embeddings for all three models across various benchmarks, with MiniCPM showing the most significant improvements of an average 56.33% performance gain. The contrastive fine-tuning code is publicly available at this https URL.
摘要：虽然大型语言模型在自然语言理解方面表现出色，但其资源密集型性质使其不太容易访问。相比之下，MiniCPM等较小的语言模型提供了更可持续的可扩展性，但如果没有专门的优化，通常表现不佳。在本文中，我们探索了通过改进文本嵌入来增强较小的语言模型。我们选择了MiniCPM、Phi-2和Gemma三种语言模型对NLI数据集进行对比微调。我们的结果表明，这种微调方法提高了所有三种模型在各种基准测试中的文本嵌入质量，其中MiniCPM表现出最显着的改进，平均性能增加了56.33%。对比微调代码可在此httpsURL上公开获取。

[NLP-6] Assessing the Variety of a Concept Space Using an Unbiased Estimate of Raos Quadratic Index
[NLP-6] 使用Raos二次指数的无偏估计评估概念空间的多样性

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00684
作者: Anubhab Majumder,Ujjwal Pal,Amaresh Chakrabarti
关键词-EN: Past research relates, Past research, relates design creativity, research relates design, divergent thinking
关键词-ZN: 过去的研究涉及，过去的研究涉及设计创造力，研究涉及设计，分歧思维
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Past research relates design creativity to ‘divergent thinking,’ i.e., how well the concept space is explored during the early phase of design. Researchers have argued that generating several concepts would increase the chances of producing better design solutions. ‘Variety’ is one of the parameters by which one can quantify the breadth of a concept space explored by the designers. It is useful to assess variety at the conceptual design stage because, at this stage, designers have the freedom to explore different solution principles so as to satisfy a design problem with substantially novel concepts. This article elaborates on and critically examines the existing variety metrics from the engineering design literature, discussing their limitations. A new distance-based variety metric is proposed, along with a prescriptive framework to support the assessment process. This framework uses the SAPPhIRE model of causality as a knowledge representation scheme to measure the real-valued distance between two design concepts. The proposed framework is implemented in a software tool called ‘VariAnT.’ Furthermore, the tool’s application is demonstrated through an illustrative example.
摘要：过去的研究将设计创造力与“发散思维”联系在一起，即在设计的早期阶段对概念空间进行探索的程度。研究人员辩称，产生几个概念将增加产生更好设计解决方案的机会。“多样性”是用来量化设计师探索的概念空间广度的参数之一。在概念设计阶段评估多样性是有用的，因为在这个阶段，设计者可以自由地探索不同的解决原则，以便用基本上新颖的概念来满足设计问题。本文详细阐述并批判性地检查了工程设计文献中现有的各种度量标准，讨论了它们的局限性。提出了一种新的基于距离的变化度量，以及一个规范的框架来支持评估过程。该框架使用Sapphire因果关系模型作为知识表示方案来度量两个设计概念之间的实值距离。建议的框架是在一个名为VariAnT的软件工具中实现的。并通过一个实例说明了该工具的应用。

[NLP-7] Leveraging Entailment Judgements in Cross-Lingual Summarisation
[NLP-7] 在跨语言总结中利用内涵判断

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00675
作者: Huajian Zhang,Laura Perez-Beltrachini
关键词-EN: Synthetically created Cross-Lingual, include document-summary pairs, Synthetically created, created Cross-Lingual Summarisation, hallucinated content
关键词-ZN: 合成创建的跨语言，包括文档摘要对，合成创建的跨语言摘要，幻觉内容
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Synthetically created Cross-Lingual Summarisation (CLS) datasets are prone to include document-summary pairs where the reference summary is unfaithful to the corresponding document as it contains content not supported by the document (i.e., hallucinated content). This low data quality misleads model learning and obscures evaluation results. Automatic ways to assess hallucinations and improve training have been proposed for monolingual summarisation, predominantly in English. For CLS, we propose to use off-the-shelf cross-lingual Natural Language Inference (X-NLI) to evaluate faithfulness of reference and model generated summaries. Then, we study training approaches that are aware of faithfulness issues in the training data and propose an approach that uses unlikelihood loss to teach a model about unfaithful summary sequences. Our results show that it is possible to train CLS models that yield more faithful summaries while maintaining comparable or better informativess.
摘要：合成创建的跨语言摘要（Collins）数据集容易包括文档摘要对，其中参考摘要与相应的文档不忠实，因为它包含文档不支持的内容（即，幻觉内容）。这种低数据质量会误导模型学习并掩盖评估结果。人们提出了评估幻觉和改善培训的自动方法，用于单语总结，主要是英语。对于CLS，我们建议使用现成的跨语言自然语言推理（X-NLI）来评估参考文献和模型生成的摘要的忠实性。然后，我们研究意识到训练数据中忠实性问题的训练方法，并提出一种使用不可能损失来教授有关不忠实摘要序列的模型的方法。我们的结果表明，可以训练具有更忠实的摘要，同时保持相当或更好的信息性。

[NLP-8] Aligning Multiple Knowledge Graphs in a Single Pass
[NLP-8] 一次对齐多个知识图

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00662
作者: Yaming Yang,Zhe Wang,Ziyu Guan,Wei Zhao,Weigang Lu,Xinyan Huang
关键词-EN: identify equivalent entities, Entity alignment, identify equivalent, knowledge graphs, KGs
关键词-ZN: 识别等效实体、实体对齐、识别等效实体、知识图、KG
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Machine Learning (cs.LG)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Entity alignment (EA) is to identify equivalent entities across different knowledge graphs (KGs), which can help fuse these KGs into a more comprehensive one. Previous EA methods mainly focus on aligning a pair of KGs, and to the best of our knowledge, no existing EA method considers aligning multiple (more than two) KGs. To fill this research gap, in this work, we study a novel problem of aligning multiple KGs and propose an effective framework named MultiEA to solve the problem. First, we embed the entities of all the candidate KGs into a common feature space by a shared KG encoder. Then, we explore three alignment strategies to minimize the distances among pre-aligned entities. In particular, we propose an innovative inference enhancement technique to improve the alignment performance by incorporating high-order similarities. Finally, to verify the effectiveness of MultiEA, we construct two new real-world benchmark datasets and conduct extensive experiments on them. The results show that our MultiEA can effectively and efficiently align multiple KGs in a single pass.
摘要：实体对齐是在不同的知识图中识别等价实体，有助于将这些知识图融合成一个更全面的知识图。以前的EA方法主要关注对齐一对KG，据我们所知，现有的EA方法没有考虑对齐多个(两个以上)KG。为了填补这一研究空白，在本文中，我们研究了一个新的多知识库对齐问题，并提出了一个有效的框架–多进化算法来解决这一问题。首先，我们通过一个共享的KG编码器将所有候选KG的实体嵌入到一个公共特征空间中。然后，我们探索了三种对齐策略来最小化预对齐实体之间的距离。特别是，我们提出了一种创新的推理增强技术，通过引入高阶相似性来提高比对性能。最后，为了验证MultiEA的有效性，我们构建了两个新的真实基准数据集，并在它们上进行了广泛的实验。结果表明，我们的多进化算法可以有效地在一次遍历中对齐多个KGS。

[NLP-9] SentenceVAE: Faster Longer and More Accurate Inference with Next-sentence Prediction for Large Language Models
[NLP-9] SentenceVAE：通过大型语言模型的下一句预测进行更快、更长、更准确的推理

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00655
作者: Hongjun An,Yifan Chen,Xiaozhen Qiao,Zhe Sun,Xuelong Li
关键词-EN: Contemporary large language, Contemporary large, large language models, predominantly utilize, next-token prediction method
关键词-ZN: 当代大型语言，当代大型语言模型，主要利用下一个令牌预测方法
类目: Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注: First preview version

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Contemporary large language models (LLMs) predominantly utilize a next-token prediction method for inference, which significantly impedes their processing speed. In this paper, we introduce a novel inference methodology termed next-sentence prediction, aimed at enhancing the inference efficiency of LLMs. We present SentenceVAE, a tiny model consisting of an encoder and a decoder. The encoder effectively condenses the information within a sentence into a singular token, while the decoder reconstructs this compressed data back into its original sentential form. By integrating SentenceVAE into the input and output layers of LLMs, we develop Sentence-level LLMs (SLLMs) that employ a sentence-by-sentence inference approach, markedly accelerating inference speeds. SentenceVAE also maintains the integrity of the original semantic content by segmenting the text into sentences, thereby preserving accuracy while boosting inference speeds. Compared to traditional LLMs, SLLMs process fewer tokens over equivalent context lengths, significantly reducing memory demands for Self-Attention computations and facilitating the handling of longer contexts. Our experimental findings reveal that this method can increase inference speeds by 204~365%, reduce perplexity (PPL) to 46~75% of its original metric, and decrease memory overhead by 86~91% for the same context length. The advantages of this approach are further amplified with increases in model parameters.
摘要：现代大型语言模型主要使用下一代词预测方法进行推理，这严重影响了它们的处理速度。本文介绍了一种新的推理方法–下一句预测，旨在提高LLMS的推理效率。我们提出了SentenceVAE，这是一个由编码器和解码器组成的微型模型。编码器有效地将句子中的信息压缩成单个令牌，而解码器将压缩的数据重建回其原始的句子形式。通过将SentenceVAE集成到LLMS的输入和输出层，我们开发了采用逐句推理方法的语句级LLMS，显著加快了推理速度。SentenceVAE还通过将文本分割成句子来维护原始语义内容的完整性，从而在提高推理速度的同时保持准确性。与传统的LLM相比，SLLM在相同的上下文长度上处理更少的令牌，显著减少了自我注意计算的内存需求，并促进了对较长上下文的处理。实验结果表明，在相同的上下文长度下，该方法可以将推理速度提高204~365%，将困惑(PPL)降低到原始度量的46~75%，并将内存开销减少86~91%。这种方法的优点随着模型参数的增加而进一步放大。

Abstract:In recent years, multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have shown strong potential in real-world applications. They are developing rapidly due to their remarkable ability to comprehend multimodal information and their inherent powerful cognitive and reasoning capabilities. Among MLLMs, vision language models (VLM) stand out for their ability to understand vision information. However, the scaling trend of VLMs under the current mainstream paradigm has not been extensively studied. Whether we can achieve better performance by training even larger models is still unclear. To address this issue, we conducted experiments on the pretraining stage of MLLMs. We conduct our experiment using different encoder sizes and large language model (LLM) sizes. [NLP-11] Downstream bias mitigation is all you need
[NLP-11] 下游偏见缓解就是您所需要的

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00612
作者: Arkadeep Baksi,Rahul Singh,Tarun Joshi
关键词-EN: natural language processing, large language models, language processing, large language, natural language
关键词-ZN: 自然语言处理、大型语言模型、语言处理、大型语言、自然语言
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注: 21 pages, 11 figures, 2 tables

点击查看摘要

Abstract:The advent of transformer-based architectures and large language models (LLMs) have significantly advanced the performance of natural language processing (NLP) models. Since these LLMs are trained on huge corpuses of data from the web and other sources, there has been a major concern about harmful prejudices that may potentially be transferred from the data. In many applications, these pre-trained LLMs are fine-tuned on task specific datasets, which can further contribute to biases. This paper studies the extent of biases absorbed by LLMs during pre-training as well as task-specific behaviour after fine-tuning. We found that controlled interventions on pre-trained LLMs, prior to fine-tuning, have minimal effect on lowering biases in classifiers. However, the biases present in domain-specific datasets play a much bigger role, and hence mitigating them at this stage has a bigger impact. While pre-training does matter, but after the model has been pre-trained, even slight changes to co-occurrence rates in the fine-tuning dataset has a significant effect on the bias of the model.
摘要：基于转换器的体系结构和大型语言模型的出现极大地提高了自然语言处理模型的性能。由于这些LLM是在来自网络和其他来源的海量数据语料库上接受培训的，因此人们主要担心可能会从数据中转移出有害的偏见。在许多应用中，这些预先训练的最小二乘法在特定于任务的数据集上进行微调，这可能会进一步导致偏差。本文研究了LLMS在训练前吸收偏差的程度，以及微调后的任务特定行为。我们发现，在微调之前，对预先训练的LLM进行受控干预，对降低分类器中的偏差的影响微乎其微。然而，特定于领域的数据集中存在的偏差发挥了更大的作用，因此在此阶段减轻它们具有更大的影响。虽然预训练确实很重要，但在模型已经预训练之后，即使微调数据集中共现率的微小变化也会对模型的偏差产生重大影响。

[NLP-12] Closing the gap between open-source and commercial large language models for medical evidence summarization
[NLP-12] 缩小医学证据总结的开源和商业大型语言模型之间的差距

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00588
作者: Gongbo Zhang,Qiao Jin,Yiliang Zhou,Song Wang,Betina R. Idnay,Yiming Luo,Elizabeth Park,Jordan G. Nestor,Matthew E. Spotnitz,Ali Soroush,Thomas Campion,Zhiyong Lu,Chunhua Weng,Yifan Peng
关键词-EN: hold great promise, Large language models, Large language, hold great, great promise
关键词-ZN: 拥有巨大的希望，大型语言模型，大型语言，拥有巨大的希望

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Large language models (LLMs) hold great promise in summarizing medical evidence. Most recent studies focus on the application of proprietary LLMs. Using proprietary LLMs introduces multiple risk factors, including a lack of transparency and vendor dependency. While open-source LLMs allow better transparency and customization, their performance falls short compared to proprietary ones. In this study, we investigated to what extent fine-tuning open-source LLMs can further improve their performance in summarizing medical evidence. Utilizing a benchmark dataset, MedReview, consisting of 8,161 pairs of systematic reviews and summaries, we fine-tuned three broadly-used, open-sourced LLMs, namely PRIMERA, LongT5, and Llama-2. Overall, the fine-tuned LLMs obtained an increase of 9.89 in ROUGE-L (95% confidence interval: 8.94-10.81), 13.21 in METEOR score (95% confidence interval: 12.05-14.37), and 15.82 in CHRF score (95% confidence interval: 13.89-16.44). The performance of fine-tuned LongT5 is close to GPT-3.5 with zero-shot settings. Furthermore, smaller fine-tuned models sometimes even demonstrated superior performance compared to larger zero-shot models. The above trends of improvement were also manifested in both human and GPT4-simulated evaluations. Our results can be applied to guide model selection for tasks demanding particular domain knowledge, such as medical evidence summarization.
摘要：大型语言模型(LLM)在总结医学证据方面有着广阔的应用前景。最近的研究主要集中在专有LLM的应用上。使用专有LLM会带来多种风险因素，包括缺乏透明度和对供应商的依赖。虽然开源LLM允许更好的透明度和定制化，但与专有LLM相比，它们的性能存在差距。在这项研究中，我们调查了微调开源LLM在多大程度上可以进一步提高它们在总结医学证据方面的性能。利用一个由8,161对系统评价和摘要组成的基准数据集MedReview，我们微调了三个广泛使用的开源LLM，即Primera、LongT5和Llama-2。总体而言，微调的LLMS在Rouge-L(95%可信区间：8.94-10.81)、流星评分(95%可信区间：12.05-14.37)和CHRF评分(95%可信区间：13.89-16.44)中获得了9.89%的增长。微调的LongT5性能接近零拍设置的GPT-3.5。此外，较小的微调模型有时甚至显示出比较大的零拍模型更优越的性能。上述改善趋势也体现在人类和GPT4模拟评估中。我们的结果可以用于指导需要特定领域知识的任务的模型选择，例如医学证据摘要。

[NLP-14] Alleviating Hallucination in Large Vision-Language Models with Active Retrieval Augmentation
[NLP-14] 通过主动检索增强减轻大型视觉语言模型中的幻觉

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00555
作者: Xiaoye Qu,Qiyuan Chen,Wei Wei,Jishuo Sun,Jianfeng Dong
关键词-EN: factually incorrect responses, frequently generate plausible, external knowledge resources, LVLM significantly lags, models frequently generate
关键词-ZN: 事实上不正确的反应，经常生成看似合理的外部知识资源，LVLM显着滞后，模型经常生成
类目: Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition (cs.CV); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Despite the remarkable ability of large vision-language models (LVLMs) in image comprehension, these models frequently generate plausible yet factually incorrect responses, a phenomenon known as hallucination.Recently, in large language models (LLMs), augmenting LLMs by retrieving information from external knowledge resources has been proven as a promising solution to mitigate hallucinations.However, the retrieval augmentation in LVLM significantly lags behind the widespread applications of LVLM. Moreover, when transferred to augmenting LVLMs, sometimes the hallucination degree of the model is even exacerbated.Motivated by the research gap and counter-intuitive phenomenon, we introduce a novel framework, the Active Retrieval-Augmented large vision-language model (ARA), specifically designed to address hallucinations by incorporating three critical dimensions: (i) dissecting the retrieval targets based on the inherent hierarchical structures of images. (ii) pinpointing the most effective retrieval methods and filtering out the reliable retrieval results. (iii) timing the retrieval process to coincide with episodes of low certainty, while circumventing unnecessary retrieval during periods of high certainty. To assess the capability of our proposed ARA model in reducing hallucination, we employ three widely used LVLM models (LLaVA-1.5, Qwen-VL, and mPLUG-Owl2) across four benchmarks. Our empirical observations suggest that by utilizing fitting retrieval mechanisms and timing the retrieval judiciously, we can effectively mitigate the hallucination problem. We hope that this study can provide deeper insights into how to adapt the retrieval augmentation to LVLMs for reducing hallucinations with more effective retrieval and minimal retrieval occurrences.
摘要：尽管大视觉语言模型在图像理解中具有显著的能力，但这些模型经常产生似是而非的错误反应，这种现象被称为幻觉。最近，在大语言模型中，通过从外部知识资源中检索信息来增强大视觉语言模型被证明是一种很有前途的解决方案，但其提取增强明显落后于大视觉语言模型的广泛应用。在研究空白和反直观现象的激励下，我们提出了一种新的框架–主动检索增强的大视觉语言模型(ARA)，该模型通过结合三个关键维度来解决幻觉问题：(I)基于图像固有的层次结构来解剖检索目标。(Ii)找出最有效的检索方法，筛选出可靠的检索结果。(3)安排检索过程与低确定性事件同时进行，同时避免在高确定性时期进行不必要的检索。为了评估我们提出的ARA模型在减少幻觉方面的能力，我们在四个基准中使用了三个广泛使用的LVLM模型(LLaVA-1.5、Qwen-VL和mPLUG-Owl2)。我们的经验观察表明，通过利用合适的提取机制和明智地选择提取时间，我们可以有效地缓解幻觉问题。我们希望这项研究能够为如何将提取增强适应于LVLMS，以更有效的提取和最少的提取次数来减少幻觉提供更深层次的见解。

[NLP-15] Mitigating Multilingual Hallucination in Large Vision-Language Models
[NLP-15] 缓解大型视觉语言模型中的多语言幻觉

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00550
作者: Xiaoye Qu,Mingyang Song,Wei Wei,Jianfeng Dong,Yu Cheng
关键词-EN: Large Vision-Language Models, Large Vision-Language, exhibited remarkable capabilities, range of tasks, exhibited remarkable

点击查看摘要

Abstract:While Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) have exhibited remarkable capabilities across a wide range of tasks, they suffer from hallucination problems, where models generate plausible yet incorrect answers given the input image-query pair. This hallucination phenomenon is even more severe when querying the image in non-English languages, while existing methods for mitigating hallucinations in LVLMs only consider the English scenarios. In this paper, we make the first attempt to mitigate this important multilingual hallucination in LVLMs. With thorough experiment analysis, we found that multilingual hallucination in LVLMs is a systemic problem that could arise from deficiencies in multilingual capabilities or inadequate multimodal abilities. To this end, we propose a two-stage Multilingual Hallucination Removal (MHR) framework for LVLMs, aiming to improve resistance to hallucination for both high-resource and low-resource languages. Instead of relying on the intricate manual annotations of multilingual resources, we fully leverage the inherent capabilities of the LVLM and propose a novel cross-lingual alignment method, which generates multiple responses for each image-query input and then identifies the hallucination-aware pairs for each language. These data pairs are finally used for direct preference optimization to prompt the LVLMs to favor non-hallucinating responses. Experimental results show that our MHR achieves a substantial reduction in hallucination generation for LVLMs. Notably, on our extended multilingual POPE benchmark, our framework delivers an average increase of 19.0% in accuracy across 13 different languages. [NLP-16] Intermittent Semi-working Mask: A New Masking Paradigm for LLMs
[NLP-16] 间歇性半工作口罩：LLM的新口罩范式

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00539
作者: Mingcong Lu,Jiangcai Zhu,Wang Hao,Zheng Li,Shusheng Zhang,Kailai Shao,Chao Chen,Nan Li,Feng Wang,Xin Lu
关键词-EN: Large Language Models, Language Models, Large Language, key interaction method, humans and Large
关键词-ZN: 大型语言模型、语言模型、大型语言、关键交互方法、人类和大型
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Multi-turn dialogues are a key interaction method between humans and Large Language Models (LLMs), as conversations extend over multiple rounds, keeping LLMs’ high generation quality and low latency is a challenge. Mainstream LLMs can be grouped into two categories based on masking strategy: causal LLM and prefix LLM. Several works have demonstrated that prefix LLMs tend to outperform causal ones in scenarios that heavily depend on historical context such as multi-turn dialogues or in-context learning, thanks to their bidirectional attention on prefix sequences. However, prefix LLMs have an inherent inefficient training problem in multi-turn dialogue datasets. In addition, the attention mechanism of prefix LLM makes it unable to reuse Key-Value Cache (KV Cache) across dialogue rounds to reduce generation latency. In this paper, we propose a novel masking scheme called Intermittent Semi-working Mask (ISM) to address these problems. Specifically, we apply alternate bidirectional and unidirectional attention on queries and answers in the dialogue history. In this way, ISM is able to maintain the high quality of prefix LLM and low generation latency of causal LLM, simultaneously. Extensive experiments illustrate that our ISM achieves significant performance.
摘要：多轮对话是人类与大型语言模型(LLMS)之间的一种关键交互方式，由于对话跨越多轮，保持LLMS的高生成质量和低延迟是一个挑战。根据掩蔽策略，主流LLM可以分为两类：因果LLM和前缀LLM。一些研究表明，前缀LLM由于对前缀序列的双向关注，在严重依赖历史语境的情景下，如多轮对话或语境中的学习，往往表现出优于因果语境的效果。然而，前缀LLMS在多话轮对话数据集中存在着训练效率低下的问题。此外，前缀LLM的注意机制使其无法跨对话轮重用键值缓存(KV缓存)来减少生成延迟。在本文中，我们提出了一种称为间歇半工作掩码(ISM)的新掩码方案来解决这些问题。具体地说，我们对对话历史中的问题和答案交替应用双向和单向关注。通过这种方式，ISM能够同时保持前缀LLM的高质量和原因LLM的低生成延迟。大量的实验表明，我们的ISM取得了显著的性能。

[NLP-17] he Monetisation of Toxicity: Analysing YouTube Content Creators and Controversy-Driven Engagement
[NLP-17] 毒性货币化：分析YouTube内容创作者和争议驱动的参与

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00534
作者: Thales Bertaglia,Catalina Goanta,Adriana Iamnitchi
关键词-EN: major social media, social media platform, digital culture, major social, social media
关键词-ZN: 主要社交媒体、社交媒体平台、数字文化、主要社交、社交媒体
类目: Computers and Society (cs.CY); Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注: Accept for publication at the 4th International Workshop on Open Challenges in Online Social Networks (OASIS) held in conjunction with 35th ACM Conference on Hypertext and Social Media (HT24)

点击查看摘要

Abstract:YouTube is a major social media platform that plays a significant role in digital culture, with content creators at its core. These creators often engage in controversial behaviour to drive engagement, which can foster toxicity. This paper presents a quantitative analysis of controversial content on YouTube, focusing on the relationship between controversy, toxicity, and monetisation. We introduce a curated dataset comprising 20 controversial YouTube channels extracted from Reddit discussions, including 16,349 videos and more than 105 million comments. We identify and categorise monetisation cues from video descriptions into various models, including affiliate marketing and direct selling, using lists of URLs and keywords. Additionally, we train a machine learning model to measure the toxicity of comments in these videos. Our findings reveal that while toxic comments correlate with higher engagement, they negatively impact monetisation, indicating that controversy-driven interaction does not necessarily lead to financial gain. We also observed significant variation in monetisation strategies, with some creators showing extensive monetisation despite high toxicity levels. Our study introduces a curated dataset, lists of URLs and keywords to categorise monetisation, a machine learning model to measure toxicity, and is a significant step towards understanding the complex relationship between controversy, engagement, and monetisation on YouTube. The lists used for detecting and categorising monetisation cues are available on this https URL.
摘要：YouTube是一个主要的社交媒体平台，在数字文化中扮演着重要的角色，内容创作者是其核心。这些创造者经常采取有争议的行为来推动参与，这可能会滋生毒性。本文对YouTube上有争议的内容进行了量化分析，重点分析了争议、毒性和货币化之间的关系。我们介绍了一个精心策划的数据集，其中包括从Reddit讨论中提取的20个有争议的YouTube频道，包括16,349个视频和超过1.05亿条评论。我们使用URL和关键字列表从视频描述中识别和分类各种模式的货币化线索，包括联属营销和直销。此外，我们还训练了一个机器学习模型来衡量这些视频中评论的毒性。我们的发现表明，尽管有毒评论与更高的参与度相关，但它们对货币化产生了负面影响，表明争议驱动的互动不一定会带来经济收益。我们还观察到货币化策略的显著差异，一些创造者表现出广泛的货币化，尽管毒性水平很高。我们的研究引入了一个精心策划的数据集、用于对货币化进行分类的URL和关键字列表、一个用于衡量毒性的机器学习模型，并且是朝着理解YouTube上的争议、参与和货币化之间的复杂关系迈出的重要一步。用于检测和分类货币化线索的列表可在此HTTPS URL上找到。

Abstract:Artwork analysis is important and fundamental skill for art appreciation, which could enrich personal aesthetic sensibility and facilitate the critical thinking ability. Understanding artworks is challenging due to its subjective nature, diverse interpretations, and complex visual elements, requiring expertise in art history, cultural background, and aesthetic theory. However, limited by the data collection and model ability, previous works for automatically analyzing artworks mainly focus on classification, retrieval, and other simple tasks, which is far from the goal of AI. To facilitate the research progress, in this paper, we step further to compose comprehensive analysis inspired by the remarkable perception and generation ability of large multimodal models. Specifically, we first propose a task of composing paragraph analysis for artworks, i.e., painting in this paper, only focusing on visual characteristics to formulate more comprehensive understanding of artworks. To support the research on formal analysis, we collect a large dataset PaintingForm, with about 19k painting images and 50k analysis paragraphs. We further introduce a superior large multimodal model for painting analysis composing, dubbed GalleryGPT, which is slightly modified and fine-tuned based on LLaVA architecture leveraging our collected data. We conduct formal analysis generation and zero-shot experiments across several datasets to assess the capacity of our model. The results show remarkable performance improvements comparing with powerful baseline LMMs, demonstrating its superb ability of art analysis and generalization. \textcolorblueThe codes and model are available at: this https URL.
摘要：艺术品分析是艺术欣赏的重要基础技能，它可以丰富个人的审美情感，促进批判性思维能力的培养。由于艺术品的主观性、多样化的解释和复杂的视觉元素，理解艺术品是具有挑战性的，需要艺术史、文化背景和美学理论方面的专业知识。然而，受数据收集和建模能力的限制，以往的艺术品自动分析工作主要集中在分类、检索等简单任务上，这与人工智能的目标相去甚远。为了促进研究的进展，本文进一步对大型多通道模型非凡的感知和生成能力进行了全面的分析。具体地说，我们首先提出了对艺术品进行段落分析的任务，即本文中的绘画，只关注视觉特征，以便对艺术品有更全面的理解。为了支持形式分析的研究，我们收集了一个大型数据集PaintingForm，大约有19k幅绘画图像和50k个分析段落。我们进一步介绍了一个用于绘画分析合成的优秀的大型多通道模型，称为GalleryGPT，该模型利用我们收集的数据，基于LLaVA架构进行了略微修改和微调。我们在几个数据集上进行了正式的分析生成和零射实验，以评估我们的模型的能力。结果表明，与强大的基准LMM相比，其性能有了显著的提高，显示了其卓越的ART分析和泛化能力。\extColBlue代码和型号可在以下网址获得：This https URL。

[NLP-19] In-Context Example Selection via Similarity Search Improves Low-Resource Machine Translation
[NLP-19] 通过相似性搜索进行上下文示例选择改进低资源机器翻译

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00397
作者: Armel Zebaze,Benoît Sagot,Rachel Bawden
关键词-EN: perform in-context learning, large language models, generative large language, natural language processing, generative large
关键词-ZN: 执行上下文学习、大型语言模型、生成式大型语言、自然语言处理、生成式大型
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:The ability of generative large language models (LLMs) to perform in-context learning has given rise to a large body of research into how best to prompt models for various natural language processing tasks. In this paper, we focus on machine translation (MT), a task that has been shown to benefit from in-context translation examples. However no systematic studies have been published on how best to select examples, and mixed results have been reported on the usefulness of similarity-based selection over random selection. We provide a study covering multiple LLMs and multiple in-context example retrieval strategies, comparing multilingual sentence embeddings. We cover several language directions, representing different levels of language resourcedness (English into French, German, Swahili and Wolof). Contrarily to previously published results, we find that sentence embedding similarity can improve MT, especially for low-resource language directions, and discuss the balance between selection pool diversity and quality. We also highlight potential problems with the evaluation of LLM-based MT and suggest a more appropriate evaluation protocol, adapting the COMET metric to the evaluation of LLMs. Code and outputs are freely available at this https URL.
摘要：生成性大语言模型(LLM)能够执行上下文中的学习，这引发了大量关于如何最好地为各种自然语言处理任务提示模型的研究。在本文中，我们将重点放在机器翻译(MT)上，这项任务已被证明受益于上下文中的翻译实例。然而，没有发表关于如何最好地选择样本的系统研究，关于基于相似性的选择比随机选择的有用性的结果好坏参半。我们提供了一项涵盖多个LLM和多个上下文中的示例检索策略的研究，比较了多语言句子嵌入。我们涵盖了几个语言方向，代表了不同水平的语言资源(将英语翻译成法语、德语、斯瓦希里语和沃尔夫语)。与前人的研究结果相反，我们发现句子嵌入相似度可以提高机器翻译，特别是对于低资源的语言方向，并讨论了选择池多样性和质量之间的平衡。我们还强调了基于LLM的MT评估的潜在问题，并建议了一个更合适的评估方案，使Comet度量适应于LLMS的评估。代码和输出可在此HTTPS URL免费获得。

Abstract:Traditional legal retrieval systems designed to retrieve legal documents, statutes, precedents, and other legal information are unable to give satisfactory answers due to lack of semantic understanding of specific questions. Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved excellent results in a variety of natural language processing tasks, which inspired us that we train a LLM in the legal domain to help legal retrieval. However, in the Chinese legal domain, due to the complexity of legal questions and the rigour of legal articles, there is no legal large model with satisfactory practical application yet. In this paper, we present DeliLaw, a Chinese legal counselling system based on a large language model. [NLP-21] ABC Align: Large Language Model Alignment for Safety Accuracy
[NLP-21] ABC Align：大型语言模型对齐以确保安全准确性

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00307
作者: Gareth Seneque,Lap-Hang Ho,Ariel Kuperman,Nafise Erfanian Saeedi,Jeffrey Molendijk
关键词-EN: Large Language Models, Large Language, Language Models, remains an unsolved, unsolved problem
关键词-ZN: 大型语言模型，大型语言，语言模型，仍然是一个未解决、未解决的问题
类目: Machine Learning (cs.LG); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注: 23 pages, 4 figures

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Alignment of Large Language Models (LLMs) remains an unsolved problem. Human preferences are highly distributed and can be captured at multiple levels of abstraction, from the individual to diverse populations. Organisational preferences, represented by standards and principles, are defined to mitigate reputational risk or meet legislative obligations. In this paper, we present ABC Align, a novel alignment methodology for LLMs that enables integration of the standards and preferences of a large media organisation into the LLM itself. We combine a set of data and methods that build on recent breakthroughs in synthetic data generation, preference optimisation, and post-training model quantisation. Our unified approach mitigates bias and improves accuracy, while preserving reasoning capability, as measured against standard benchmarks.
摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）的对齐仍然是一个未解决的问题。人类的偏好高度分布，可以在多个抽象水平上捕捉，从个人到多样化的人群。以标准和原则为代表的组织偏好的定义是为了减轻声誉风险或履行立法义务。在本文中，我们介绍了ABC Align，这是一种针对LLM的新型调整方法，可以将大型媒体组织的标准和偏好集成到LLM本身中。我们结合了一组数据和方法，这些数据和方法建立在合成数据生成、偏好优化和训练后模型量化方面的最新突破的基础上。我们的统一方法减轻了偏见并提高了准确性，同时保留了根据标准基准衡量的推理能力。

Abstract:Large-scale text-to-speech (TTS) models have made significant progress recently.However, they still fall short in the generation of Chinese dialectal speech. Toaddress this, we propose Bailing-TTS, a family of large-scale TTS models capable of generating high-quality Chinese dialectal speech. Bailing-TTS serves as a foundation model for Chinese dialectal speech generation. First, continual semi-supervised learning is proposed to facilitate the alignment of text tokens and speech tokens. Second, the Chinese dialectal representation learning is developed using a specific transformer architecture and multi-stage training processes. With the proposed design of novel network architecture and corresponding strategy, Bailing-TTS is able to generate Chinese dialectal speech from text effectively and efficiently. [NLP-24] QUITO: Accelerating Long-Context Reasoning through Query-Guided Context Compression
[NLP-24] QUito：通过查询引导上下文压缩加速长上下文推理

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00274
作者: Wenshan Wang,Yihang Wang,Yixing Fan,Huaming Liao,Jiafeng Guo
关键词-EN: large language models, In-context learning, capabilities are foundational, language models, success of large
关键词-ZN: 大型语言模型、上下文学习、能力是基础、语言模型、大型的成功
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:In-context learning (ICL) capabilities are foundational to the success of large language models (LLMs). Recently, context compression has attracted growing interest since it can largely reduce reasoning complexities and computation costs of LLMs. In this paper, we introduce a novel Query-gUIded aTtention cOmpression (QUITO) method, which leverages attention of the question over the contexts to filter useless information. Specifically, we take a trigger token to calculate the attention distribution of the context in response to the question. Based on the distribution, we propose three different filtering methods to satisfy the budget constraints of the context length. We evaluate the QUITO using two widely-used datasets, namely, NaturalQuestions and ASQA. Experimental results demonstrate that QUITO significantly outperforms established baselines across various datasets and downstream LLMs, underscoring its effectiveness. Our code is available at this https URL.
摘要：上下文学习（ICL）能力是大型语言模型（LLM）成功的基础。最近，上下文压缩引起了越来越多的兴趣，因为它可以大大降低LLM的推理复杂性和计算成本。在本文中，我们引入了一种新型的查询gUIded aTintence cEmption（QUito）方法，该方法利用对问题的关注来过滤无用的信息。具体来说，我们采用触发令牌来计算上下文响应问题的注意力分布。基于这种分布，我们提出了三种不同的过滤方法来满足上下文长度的预算限制。我们使用两个广泛使用的数据集（即NaturalQuestions和ASQA）来评估QUito。实验结果表明，QUito的表现显着优于各种数据集和下游LLM的既定基线，凸显了其有效性。我们的代码可在此https URL上找到。

[NLP-25] Clover-2: Accurate Inference for Regressive Lightweight Speculative Decoding
[NLP-25] Clover-2：回归轻量级投机解码的准确推断

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00264
作者: Bin Xiao,Lujun Gui,Lei Su,Weipeng Chen
关键词-EN: Large Language Models, Large Language, Recurrent Neural Network, Language Models, frequently suffer
关键词-ZN: 大型语言模型、大型语言、循环神经网络、语言模型，经常受到影响
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Machine Learning (cs.LG)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Large Language Models (LLMs) frequently suffer from inefficiencies, largely attributable to the discord between the requirements of auto-regressive decoding and the architecture of contemporary GPUs. Recently, regressive lightweight speculative decoding has garnered attention for its notable efficiency improvements in text generation tasks. This approach utilizes a lightweight regressive draft model, like a Recurrent Neural Network (RNN) or a single transformer decoder layer, leveraging sequential information to iteratively predict potential tokens. Specifically, RNN draft models are computationally economical but tend to deliver lower accuracy, while attention decoder layer models exhibit the opposite traits. This paper presents Clover-2, an advanced iteration of Clover, an RNN-based draft model designed to achieve comparable accuracy to that of attention decoder layer models while maintaining minimal computational overhead. Clover-2 enhances the model architecture and incorporates knowledge distillation to increase Clover’s accuracy and improve overall efficiency. We conducted experiments using the open-source Vicuna 7B and LLaMA3-Instruct 8B models. The results demonstrate that Clover-2 surpasses existing methods across various model architectures, showcasing its efficacy and robustness.
摘要：大型语言模型经常存在效率低下的问题，这在很大程度上是由于自回归解码的要求与当代GPU体系结构之间的不协调造成的。最近，回归轻量级推测译码因其在文本生成任务中的显著效率提高而受到关注。该方法利用轻量级回归草稿模型，如递归神经网络(RNN)或单个变压器解码器层，利用顺序信息迭代地预测潜在的令牌。具体地说，RNN草稿模型在计算上是经济的，但往往提供较低的精度，而注意解码层模型表现出相反的特征。本文提出了CLOVER-2，它是CLOVER的高级迭代，是一种基于RNN的草稿模型，旨在获得与注意解码层模型相当的精度，同时保持最小的计算开销。三叶草-2增强了模型架构，并加入了知识蒸馏，以提高三叶草的准确性和整体效率。我们使用开源的维古纳7B和LLaMA3-指令8B模型进行了实验。结果表明，CLOVER-2在不同的模型体系结构上都优于已有的方法，显示了其有效性和健壮性。

[NLP-26] Enhanced Structured State Space Models via Grouped FIR Filtering and Attention Sink Mechanisms
[NLP-26] 通过成组有限责任区过滤和注意力下沉机制增强的结构化状态空间模型

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00244
作者: Tian Meng,Yang Tao,Wuliang Yin
关键词-EN: Structured State Space, State Space Models, Structured State, State Space, offering linear-time complexity
关键词-ZN: 结构化状态空间，状态空间模型，结构化状态，状态空间，提供线性时间复杂性
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Machine Learning (cs.LG)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Structured State Space Models (SSMs) have emerged as compelling alternatives to Transformer architectures, offering linear-time complexity and superior performance in various sequence modeling tasks. Despite their advantages, SSMs like the original Mamba-2 face training difficulties due to the sensitivities introduced by the extended series of recurrent matrix multiplications. In this paper, we propose an advanced architecture that mitigates these challenges by decomposing A-multiplications into multiple groups and optimizing positional encoding through Grouped Finite Impulse Response (FIR) filtering. This new structure, denoted as Grouped FIR-enhanced SSM (GFSSM), employs semiseparable matrices for efficient computation. Furthermore, inspired by the “attention sink” phenomenon identified in streaming language models, we incorporate a similar mechanism to enhance the stability and performance of our model over extended sequences. Our approach further bridges the gap between SSMs and Transformer architectures, offering a viable path forward for scalable and high-performing sequence modeling.
摘要：结构化状态空间模型(SSM)已经成为变压器体系结构的引人注目的替代方案，在各种序列建模任务中提供了线性时间复杂性和优异的性能。尽管它们具有优势，但像最初的MAMBA-2这样的SSM由于扩展的递归矩阵乘法系列引入的敏感性而面临训练困难。在本文中，我们提出了一种先进的体系结构，通过将A乘法分解成多个组并通过分组有限脉冲响应(FIR)滤波来优化位置编码来缓解这些挑战。这种新的结构被称为分组FIR增强SSM(GFSSM)，它使用半可分离矩阵来进行有效的计算。此外，受流媒体语言模型中发现的“注意力下沉”现象的启发，我们引入了类似的机制来增强我们的模型在扩展序列上的稳定性和性能。我们的方法进一步弥合了SSM和Transformer体系结构之间的差距，为可扩展和高性能的序列建模提供了一条可行的途径。

[NLP-27] Lost in Translation: Latent Concept Misalignment in Text-to-Image Diffusion Models
[NLP-27] 迷失在翻译中：文本到图像扩散模型中潜在的概念失调

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00230
作者: Juntu Zhao,Junyu Deng,Yixin Ye,Chongxuan Li,Zhijie Deng,Dequan Wang
关键词-EN: downstream practical applications, broadened extensive downstream, extensive downstream practical, encounter misalignment issues, iced coke
关键词-ZN: 下游实际应用，拓宽广泛的下游，广泛的下游实际，遇到未对准问题，冰焦
类目: Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Computation and Language (cs.CL)
备注: 33 pages, 19 figures

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Advancements in text-to-image diffusion models have broadened extensive downstream practical applications, but such models often encounter misalignment issues between text and image. Taking the generation of a combination of two disentangled concepts as an example, say given the prompt “a tea cup of iced coke”, existing models usually generate a glass cup of iced coke because the iced coke usually co-occurs with the glass cup instead of the tea one during model training. The root of such misalignment is attributed to the confusion in the latent semantic space of text-to-image diffusion models, and hence we refer to the “a tea cup of iced coke” phenomenon as Latent Concept Misalignment (LC-Mis). We leverage large language models (LLMs) to thoroughly investigate the scope of LC-Mis, and develop an automated pipeline for aligning the latent semantics of diffusion models to text prompts. Empirical assessments confirm the effectiveness of our approach, substantially reducing LC-Mis errors and enhancing the robustness and versatility of text-to-image diffusion models. Our code and dataset have been available online for reference.
摘要：文本到图像扩散模型的进步拓宽了下游的实际应用，但此类模型经常会遇到文本和图像之间的不对准问题。以两个解开的概念组合的生成为例，假设给出提示“一杯冰可乐”，现有的模型通常会生成一杯冰可乐，因为在模型训练期间，冰可乐通常与玻璃杯而不是茶杯同时出现。这种错位的根源在于文本到图像扩散模型的潜在语义空间中的混乱，因此我们称之为潜在概念错位(LC-Mis)。我们利用大型语言模型(LLMS)来彻底调查LC-MI的范围，并开发一条自动管道来将扩散模型的潜在语义与文本提示对齐。实验评估证实了我们方法的有效性，大大减少了LC-MIS误差，并增强了文本到图像扩散模型的稳健性和通用性。我们的代码和数据集已在网上提供参考。

[NLP-28] Sentence-wise Speech Summarization: Task Datasets and End-to-End Modeling with LM Knowledge Distillation INTERSPEECH2024
[NLP-28] 逐句语音摘要：任务数据集和使用LM知识提炼的端到端建模

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00205
作者: Kohei Matsuura,Takanori Ashihara,Takafumi Moriya,Masato Mimura,Takatomo Kano,Atsunori Ogawa,Marc Delcroix
关键词-EN: called sentence-wise speech, approach called sentence-wise, generates text summaries, sentence-wise speech summarization, paper introduces
关键词-ZN: 所谓的情景语音，称为情景语音，生成文本摘要，情景语音摘要，论文介绍
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Audio and Speech Processing (eess.AS)
备注: Accepted to Interspeech2024. Dataset: this https URL

点击查看摘要

Abstract:This paper introduces a novel approach called sentence-wise speech summarization (Sen-SSum), which generates text summaries from a spoken document in a sentence-by-sentence manner. Sen-SSum combines the real-time processing of automatic speech recognition (ASR) with the conciseness of speech summarization. To explore this approach, we present two datasets for Sen-SSum: Mega-SSum and CSJ-SSum. Using these datasets, our study evaluates two types of Transformer-based models: 1) cascade models that combine ASR and strong text summarization models, and 2) end-to-end (E2E) models that directly convert speech into a text summary. While E2E models are appealing to develop compute-efficient models, they perform worse than cascade models. Therefore, we propose knowledge distillation for E2E models using pseudo-summaries generated by the cascade models. Our experiments show that this proposed knowledge distillation effectively improves the performance of the E2E model on both datasets.
摘要：本文介绍了一种名为按句子顺序语音摘要（Sen-Ssum）的新颖方法，该方法以逐句方式从语音文档生成文本摘要。Sen-Ssum将自动语音识别（ASB）的实时处理与语音摘要的简洁性相结合。为了探索这种方法，我们为Sen-SSum提供了两个数据集：Mega-SSum和CSJ-SSum。使用这些数据集，我们的研究评估了两种类型的基于Transformer的模型：1）结合了ASB和强文本摘要模型的级联模型，以及2）直接将语音转换为文本摘要的端到端（E2 E）模型。虽然E2 E模型吸引人们开发计算效率高的模型，但它们的性能比级联模型更差。因此，我们提出使用级联模型生成的伪摘要对E2 E模型进行知识提炼。我们的实验表明，这种提出的知识提炼有效地提高了E2 E模型在两个数据集上的性能。

[NLP-29] OmniParser for Pure Vision Based GUI Agent
[NLP-29] OmniParser用于基于纯视觉的图形用户界面代理

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00203
作者: Yadong Lu,Jianwei Yang,Yelong Shen,Ahmed Awadallah
关键词-EN: large vision language, shows great potential, vision language models, language models shows, models shows great
关键词-ZN: 大视觉语言，显示出巨大的潜力，视觉语言模型，语言模型显示，模型显示伟大
类目: Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition (cs.CV); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Computation and Language (cs.CL); Machine Learning (cs.LG)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:The recent success of large vision language models shows great potential in driving the agent system operating on user interfaces. However, we argue that the power multimodal models like GPT-4V as a general agent on multiple operating systems across different applications is largely underestimated due to the lack of a robust screen parsing technique capable of: 1) reliably identifying interactable icons within the user interface, and 2) understanding the semantics of various elements in a screenshot and accurately associate the intended action with the corresponding region on the screen. To fill these gaps, we introduce \textscOmniParser, a comprehensive method for parsing user interface screenshots into structured elements, which significantly enhances the ability of GPT-4V to generate actions that can be accurately grounded in the corresponding regions of the interface. We first curated an interactable icon detection dataset using popular webpages and an icon description dataset. These datasets were utilized to fine-tune specialized models: a detection model to parse interactable regions on the screen and a caption model to extract the functional semantics of the detected elements. \textscOmniParser significantly improves GPT-4V’s performance on ScreenSpot benchmark. And on Mind2Web and AITW benchmark, \textscOmniParser with screenshot only input outperforms the GPT-4V baselines requiring additional information outside of screenshot.
摘要：最近大型视觉语言模型的成功显示了在驱动用户界面上操作的代理系统方面的巨大潜力。然而，我们认为，像GPT-4V这样的强大的多模式模型作为跨不同应用程序的多个操作系统的总代理在很大程度上被低估了，因为缺乏强大的屏幕解析技术，该技术能够：1)可靠地识别用户界面内的可交互图标；2)理解屏幕截图中各种元素的语义，并准确地将预期操作与屏幕上的相应区域相关联。为了填补这些空白，我们引入了\extscOmniParser，这是一种将用户界面截图解析为结构化元素的综合方法，它显著增强了GPT-4V生成可准确植根于界面相应区域的操作的能力。我们首先使用流行网页和图标描述数据集创建了一个可交互的图标检测数据集。这些数据集被用来微调专门的模型：一个用于解析屏幕上可交互区域的检测模型和一个用于提取所检测元素的功能语义的字幕模型。\textscOmniParser显著提高了GPT-4V在ScreenSpot基准上的性能。在Mind2Web和AITW Benchmark上，只输入屏幕截图的\extscOmniParser性能优于GPT-4V基线，需要屏幕截图以外的额外信息。

[NLP-30] Automated Software Vulnerability Static Code Analysis Using Generative Pre-Trained Transformer Models
[NLP-30] 使用生成式预训练Transformer模型的自动化软件漏洞静态代码分析

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00197
作者: Elijah Pelofske,Vincent Urias,Lorie M. Liebrock
关键词-EN: Generative Pre-Trained Transformer, Pre-Trained Transformer models, including generating computer, generating computer code, language processing tasks
关键词-ZN: 生成式预训练Transformer、预训练Transformer模型，包括生成计算机、生成计算机代码、语言处理任务
类目: Cryptography and Security (cs.CR); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Computation and Language (cs.CL); Machine Learning (cs.LG)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Generative Pre-Trained Transformer models have been shown to be surprisingly effective at a variety of natural language processing tasks – including generating computer code. We evaluate the effectiveness of open source GPT models for the task of automatic identification of the presence of vulnerable code syntax (specifically targeting C and C++ source code). This task is evaluated on a selection of 36 source code examples from the NIST SARD dataset, which are specifically curated to not contain natural English that indicates the presence, or lack thereof, of a particular vulnerability. The NIST SARD source code dataset contains identified vulnerable lines of source code that are examples of one out of the 839 distinct Common Weakness Enumerations (CWE), allowing for exact quantification of the GPT output classification error rate. A total of 5 GPT models are evaluated, using 10 different inference temperatures and 100 repetitions at each setting, resulting in 5,000 GPT queries per vulnerable source code analyzed. Ultimately, we find that the GPT models that we evaluated are not suitable for fully automated vulnerability scanning because the false positive and false negative rates are too high to likely be useful in practice. However, we do find that the GPT models perform surprisingly well at automated vulnerability detection for some of the test cases, in particular surpassing random sampling, and being able to identify the exact lines of code that are vulnerable albeit at a low success rate. The best performing GPT model result found was Llama-2-70b-chat-hf with inference temperature of 0.1 applied to NIST SARD test case 149165 (which is an example of a buffer overflow vulnerability), which had a binary classification recall score of 1.0 and a precision of 1.0 for correctly and uniquely identifying the vulnerable line of code and the correct CWE number.
摘要：生成性预先训练的Transformer模型已经被证明在各种自然语言处理任务中出人意料地有效–包括生成计算机代码。我们评估了开源GPT模型在自动识别存在的易受攻击代码语法(特别是针对C和C++源代码)任务中的有效性。这项任务是根据从NIST SARD数据集中选择的36个源代码示例进行评估的，这些示例经过专门策划，不包含指示特定漏洞存在或不存在的自然英语。NIST SARD源代码数据集包含已识别的易受攻击的源代码行，这些代码行是839个不同的常见弱点枚举(CWE)中的一个，从而可以准确量化GPT输出分类错误率。总共评估了5个GPT模型，使用10个不同的推理温度和每个设置的100个重复，导致每个分析的易受攻击的源代码有5,000个GPT查询。最终，我们发现我们评估的GPT模型不适合全自动漏洞扫描，因为误报和漏检率太高，不太可能在实践中有用。然而，我们确实发现，GPT模型在一些测试用例的自动漏洞检测方面表现得出人意料地好，特别是超过了随机抽样，并能够识别出尽管成功率较低但仍易受攻击的确切代码行。发现的性能最好的GPT模型结果是Llama-2-70b-Chat-HF，推理温度为0.1，应用于NIST SARD测试用例149165(这是缓冲区溢出漏洞的一个示例)，其二进制分类召回分数为1.0，精度为1.0，用于正确和唯一地识别易受攻击的代码行和正确的CWE编号。

[NLP-31] A Taxonomy of Stereotype Content in Large Language Models
[NLP-31] 大型语言模型中刻板印象内容的分类

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00162
作者: Gandalf Nicolas,Aylin Caliskan
关键词-EN: large language models, contemporary large language, language models, study introduces, contemporary large
关键词-ZN: 大型语言模型，当代大型语言，语言模型，研究介绍，当代大型
类目: Computers and Society (cs.CY); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Computation and Language (cs.CL); Machine Learning (cs.LG)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:This study introduces a taxonomy of stereotype content in contemporary large language models (LLMs). We prompt ChatGPT 3.5, Llama 3, and Mixtral 8x7B, three powerful and widely used LLMs, for the characteristics associated with 87 social categories (e.g., gender, race, occupations). We identify 14 stereotype dimensions (e.g., Morality, Ability, Health, Beliefs, Emotions), accounting for ~90% of LLM stereotype associations. Warmth and Competence facets were the most frequent content, but all other dimensions were significantly prevalent. Stereotypes were more positive in LLMs (vs. humans), but there was significant variability across categories and dimensions. Finally, the taxonomy predicted the LLMs’ internal evaluations of social categories (e.g., how positively/negatively the categories were represented), supporting the relevance of a multidimensional taxonomy for characterizing LLM stereotypes. Our findings suggest that high-dimensional human stereotypes are reflected in LLMs and must be considered in AI auditing and debiasing to minimize unidentified harms from reliance in low-dimensional views of bias in LLMs.
摘要：本研究对当代大型语言模型中的刻板印象内容进行了分类。我们建议ChatGPT 3.5、Llama 3和Mixtral 8x7B这三个功能强大且广泛使用的LLM，用于描述与87个社会类别(例如，性别、种族、职业)相关的特征。我们确定了14个刻板印象维度(例如，道德、能力、健康、信仰、情感)，占LLM刻板印象关联的90%左右。温暖和能力方面是最常见的内容，但所有其他维度都非常普遍。刻板印象在LLM(与人类相比)中更积极，但在不同类别和维度之间存在显著差异。最后，分类法预测了LLMS对社会类别的内部评估(例如，这些类别被代表的正面/负面程度)，支持了多维分类对表征LLM刻板印象的相关性。我们的发现表明，高维度的人类刻板印象反映在LLM中，在人工智能审计和去偏见中必须考虑到这一点，以最大限度地减少依赖于LLM中的低维度偏见的低维观点造成的不明伤害。

[NLP-32] Automatic Generation of Behavioral Test Cases For Natural Language Processing Using Clustering and Prompting
[NLP-32] 使用集群和预算分配自动生成自然语言处理的行为测试用例

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00161
作者: Ying Li,Rahul Singh,Tarun Joshi,Agus Sudjianto
关键词-EN: software engineering testing, Recent work, natural language processing, engineering testing, inspired by related
关键词-ZN: 软件工程测试，最近的工作，自然语言处理，工程测试，灵感来自相关
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI); Emerging Technologies (cs.ET); Machine Learning (cs.LG)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Recent work in behavioral testing for natural language processing (NLP) models, such as Checklist, is inspired by related paradigms in software engineering testing. They allow evaluation of general linguistic capabilities and domain understanding, hence can help evaluate conceptual soundness and identify model weaknesses. However, a major challenge is the creation of test cases. The current packages rely on semi-automated approach using manual development which requires domain expertise and can be time consuming. This paper introduces an automated approach to develop test cases by exploiting the power of large language models and statistical techniques. It clusters the text representations to carefully construct meaningful groups and then apply prompting techniques to automatically generate Minimal Functionality Tests (MFT). The well-known Amazon Reviews corpus is used to demonstrate our approach. We analyze the behavioral test profiles across four different classification algorithms and discuss the limitations and strengths of those models.
摘要：最近在自然语言处理(NLP)模型的行为测试方面的工作，如Checklist，是受到软件工程测试中相关范例的启发。它们允许评估一般的语言能力和领域理解，因此可以帮助评估概念的合理性和识别模型的弱点。然而，一个主要的挑战是测试用例的创建。目前的包依赖于使用手动开发的半自动方法，这需要领域专业知识，而且可能很耗时。本文介绍了一种利用大型语言模型和统计技术的能力来自动开发测试用例的方法。它对文本表示进行聚类以仔细构建有意义的组，然后应用提示技术自动生成最小功能测试(MFT)。我们使用了著名的亚马逊评论语料库来演示我们的方法。我们分析了四种不同分类算法的行为测试配置文件，并讨论了这些模型的局限性和优势。

[NLP-33] Distributed In-Context Learning under Non-IID Among Clients
[NLP-33] 客户之间非IID下的分布式上下文学习

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00144
作者: Siqi Liang,Sumyeong Ahn,Jiayu Zhou
关键词-EN: complicated natural language, natural language reasoning, language reasoning tasks, large language models, Advancements in large
关键词-ZN: 复杂的自然语言、自然语言推理、语言推理任务、大型语言模型、大型进步
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI)
备注: 12 pages

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Advancements in large language models (LLMs) have shown their effectiveness in multiple complicated natural language reasoning tasks. A key challenge remains in adapting these models efficiently to new or unfamiliar tasks. In-context learning (ICL) provides a promising solution for few-shot adaptation by retrieving a set of data points relevant to a query, called in-context examples (ICE), from a training dataset and providing them during the inference as context. Most existing studies utilize a centralized training dataset, yet many real-world datasets may be distributed among multiple clients, and remote data retrieval can be associated with costs. Especially when the client data are non-identical independent distributions (non-IID), retrieving from clients a proper set of ICEs needed for a test query presents critical challenges. In this paper, we first show that in this challenging setting, test queries will have different preferences among clients because of non-IIDness, and equal contribution often leads to suboptimal performance. We then introduce a novel approach to tackle the distributed non-IID ICL problem when a data usage budget is present. The principle is that each client’s proper contribution (budget) should be designed according to the preference of each query for that client. Our approach uses a data-driven manner to allocate a budget for each client, tailored to each test query. Through extensive empirical studies on diverse datasets, our framework demonstrates superior performance relative to competing baselines.
摘要：大型语言模型在复杂自然语言推理任务中的应用取得了很好的效果。一个关键的挑战仍然是如何有效地使这些模型适应新的或不熟悉的任务。上下文中学习(ICL)通过从训练数据集中检索一组与查询相关的数据点，称为上下文中示例(ICE)，并在推理过程中将它们作为上下文提供，从而为少机会适应提供了一种有前途的解决方案。大多数现有的研究使用集中的训练数据集，然而许多真实世界的数据集可能分布在多个客户端，并且远程数据检索可能与成本相关联。特别是当客户端数据是不相同的独立分布(非IID)时，从客户端检索测试查询所需的适当ICE集合是一个关键挑战。在本文中，我们首先证明了在这种具有挑战性的环境中，测试查询会因为非IID而在不同的客户之间有不同的偏好，相同的贡献往往会导致次优的性能。然后，我们介绍了一种新的方法来解决存在数据使用预算时的分布式非IID ICL问题。原则是，每个客户的适当捐款(预算)应根据该客户的每个查询的偏好来设计。我们的方法使用数据驱动的方式为每个客户端分配预算，为每个测试查询量身定做。通过对不同数据集的广泛实证研究，我们的框架显示出相对于竞争基线的优越性能。

[NLP-34] Correcting Negative Bias in Large Language Models through Negative Attention Score Alignment
[NLP-34] 通过负注意力分数对齐纠正大型语言模型中的负偏见

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00137
作者: Sangwon Yu,Jongyoon Song,Bongkyu Hwang,Hoyoung Kang,Sooah Cho,Junhwa Choi,Seongho Joe,Taehee Lee,Youngjune L. Gwon,Sungroh Yoon
关键词-EN: significant real-world scenario, binary decision task, negative bias, reflects a significant, specific issues
关键词-ZN: 重要的现实世界场景、二元决策任务、消极偏见，反映了一个重要的具体问题
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI)
备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:A binary decision task, like yes-no questions or answer verification, reflects a significant real-world scenario such as where users look for confirmation about the correctness of their decisions on specific issues. In this work, we observe that language models exhibit a negative bias in the binary decisions of complex reasoning tasks. Based on our observations and the rationale about attention-based model dynamics, we propose a negative attention score (NAS) to systematically and quantitatively formulate negative bias. Based on NAS, we identify attention heads that attend to negative tokens provided in the instructions as answer candidate of binary decisions, regardless of the question in the prompt, and validate their association with the negative bias. Additionally, we propose the negative attention score alignment (NASA) method, which is a parameter-efficient fine-tuning technique to address the extracted negatively biased attention heads. Experimental results from various domains of reasoning tasks and large model search space demonstrate that NASA significantly reduces the gap between precision and recall caused by negative bias while preserving their generalization abilities. Our codes are available at \urlthis https URL.
摘要：二元决策任务，如是非问题或答案验证，反映了一个重要的现实世界场景，例如用户希望确认他们在特定问题上决策的正确性。在这项工作中，我们观察到语言模型在复杂推理任务的二元决策中表现出负偏差。基于我们的观察和基于注意的模型动力学的基本原理，我们提出了负注意分数(NAS)来系统地、定量地表示负偏差。基于NAS，我们将注意到指令中提供的否定标记的注意中心识别为二元决策的候选答案，而不考虑提示中的问题，并验证它们与否定偏向的关联。此外，我们还提出了负注意分数对齐(NASA)方法，这是一种参数高效的微调技术，用于处理提取的负偏向注意头部。在不同领域的推理任务和大的模型搜索空间上的实验结果表明，NASA在保持其泛化能力的同时，显著地缩小了由于负偏差而导致的查准率和召回率之间的差距。我们的代码可在此HTTPS URL上找到。

Abstract:In this work, we introduce Gemma 2, a new addition to the Gemma family of lightweight, state-of-the-art open models, ranging in scale from 2 billion to 27 billion parameters. [NLP-37] Measuring Progress in Dictionary Learning for Language Model Interpretability with Board Game Models ICML2024
[NLP-37] 使用棋盘游戏模型衡量语言模型可解释性词典学习的进展

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00113
作者: Adam Karvonen,Benjamin Wright,Can Rager,Rico Angell,Jannik Brinkmann,Logan Smith,Claudio Mayrink Verdun,David Bau,Samuel Marks
关键词-EN: language model, encoded in language, interpretable features, interpretable, features
关键词-ZN: 语言模型，用语言编码，可解释特征，可解释，特征

备注: Oral paper (top 5%) at the ICML 2024 Mechanistic Interpretability Workshop

点击查看摘要

Abstract:What latent features are encoded in language model (LM) representations? Recent work on training sparse autoencoders (SAEs) to disentangle interpretable features in LM representations has shown significant promise. However, evaluating the quality of these SAEs is difficult because we lack a ground-truth collection of interpretable features that we expect good SAEs to recover. We thus propose to measure progress in interpretable dictionary learning by working in the setting of LMs trained on chess and Othello transcripts. These settings carry natural collections of interpretable features – for example, “there is a knight on F3” – which we leverage into \textitsupervised metrics for SAE quality. To guide progress in interpretable dictionary learning, we introduce a new SAE training technique, \textitp-annealing , which improves performance on prior unsupervised metrics as well as our new metrics.
摘要：语言模型（LM）表示中编码了哪些潜在特征？最近关于训练稀疏自动编码器（SAEs）以解开LM表示中的可解释特征的工作显示出了巨大的前景。然而，评估这些严重不良事件的质量很困难，因为我们缺乏可解释特征的基本事实收集，我们希望良好的严重不良事件能够恢复。因此，我们建议通过在国际象棋和奥赛罗成绩单上训练的LM环境中工作来衡量可解释词典学习的进展。这些设置携带可解释特征的自然集合–例如，“F3上有一个骑士”–我们将其利用到\textitsupervised指标中来测量严重不良事件质量。为了指导可解释词典学习的进展，我们引入了一种新的SAGE训练技术\textitp-annealing，它可以提高先前无监督指标以及我们的新指标的性能。

[NLP-38] ReLiK: Retrieve and LinK Fast and Accurate Entity Linking and Relation Extraction on an Academic Budget ACL2024
[NLP-38] ReLiK：Inbox和LinkK快速准确的实体链接和学术预算的关系提取

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00103
作者: Riccardo Orlando,Pere-Lluis Huguet-Cabot,Edoardo Barba,Roberto Navigli
关键词-EN: Natural Language Processing, Entity Linking, tasks in Natural, Language Processing, Natural Language
关键词-ZN: 自然语言处理、实体链接、自然任务、语言处理、自然语言
类目: Computation and Language (cs.CL); Artificial Intelligence (cs.AI)
备注: To be presented at ACL 2024

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Entity Linking (EL) and Relation Extraction (RE) are fundamental tasks in Natural Language Processing, serving as critical components in a wide range of applications. In this paper, we propose ReLiK, a Retriever-Reader architecture for both EL and RE, where, given an input text, the Retriever module undertakes the identification of candidate entities or relations that could potentially appear within the text. Subsequently, the Reader module is tasked to discern the pertinent retrieved entities or relations and establish their alignment with the corresponding textual spans. Notably, we put forward an innovative input representation that incorporates the candidate entities or relations alongside the text, making it possible to link entities or extract relations in a single forward pass and to fully leverage pre-trained language models contextualization capabilities, in contrast with previous Retriever-Reader-based methods, which require a forward pass for each candidate. Our formulation of EL and RE achieves state-of-the-art performance in both in-domain and out-of-domain benchmarks while using academic budget training and with up to 40x inference speed compared to competitors. Finally, we show how our architecture can be used seamlessly for Information Extraction (cIE), i.e. EL + RE, and setting a new state of the art by employing a shared Reader that simultaneously extracts entities and relations.
摘要：实体链接(EL)和关系抽取(RE)是自然语言处理中的基本任务，在广泛的应用中起着至关重要的作用。在本文中，我们提出了一种用于EL和RE的Retriever-Reader体系结构Relik，其中，给定一个输入文本，Retriever模块负责识别可能出现在文本中的候选实体或关系。随后，阅读器模块的任务是辨别相关的检索到的实体或关系，并建立它们与相应的文本跨度的对齐。值得注意的是，我们提出了一种创新的输入表示法，它将候选实体或关系与文本结合在一起，使之能够在单一的前向传递中链接实体或提取关系，并充分利用预先训练的语言模型的上下文能力，而以前的基于Retriever-Reader的方法需要为每个候选人提供前向传递。我们的EL和RE公式在域内和域外基准测试中都实现了最先进的性能，同时使用了学术预算培训，与竞争对手相比，推理速度高达40倍。最后，我们展示了我们的体系结构如何无缝地用于信息提取(CIE)，即EL+RE，并通过使用同时提取实体和关系的共享阅读器来设置新的技术状态。

[NLP-39] SynesLM: A Unified Approach for Audio-visual Speech Recognition and Translation via Language Model and Synthetic Data
[NLP-39] SynesLM：通过语言模型和合成数据进行视听语音识别和翻译的统一方法

Abstract:In this work, we present SynesLM, an unified model which can perform three multimodal language understanding tasks: audio-visual automatic speech recognition(AV-ASR) and visual-aided speech/machine translation(VST/VMT). Unlike previous research that focused on lip motion as visual cues for speech signals, our work explores more general visual information within entire frames, such as objects and actions. Additionally, we use synthetic image data to enhance the correlation between image and speech data. We benchmark SynesLM against the How2 dataset, demonstrating performance on par with state-of-the-art (SOTA) models dedicated to AV-ASR while maintaining our multitasking framework. Remarkably, for zero-shot AV-ASR, SynesLM achieved SOTA performance by lowering the Word Error Rate (WER) from 43.4% to 39.4% on the VisSpeech Dataset. Furthermore, our results in VST and VMT outperform the previous results, improving the BLEU score to 43.5 from 37.2 for VST, and to 54.8 from 54.4 for VMT.

[NLP-40] owards a Universal Method for Meaningful Signal Detection
[NLP-40] 拥有一种通用的有意义信号检测方法

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00016
作者: Louis Mahon
关键词-EN: convey meaningful content, convey meaningful, meaningful content, decipher the content, utterance does convey
关键词-ZN: 传达有意义的内容，传达有意义的内容，破译内容，话语确实传达

备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:It is known that human speech and certain animal vocalizations can convey meaningful content because we can decipher the content that a given utterance does convey. This paper explores an alternative approach to determining whether a signal is meaningful, one that analyzes only the signal itself and is independent of what the conveyed meaning might be. We devise a method that takes a waveform as input and outputs a score indicating its degree of meaningfulness. We cluster contiguous portions of the input to minimize the total description length, and then take the length of the code of the assigned cluster labels as meaningfulness score. We evaluate our method empirically, against several baselines, and show that it is the only one to give a high score to human speech in various languages and with various speakers, a moderate score to animal vocalizations from birds and orcas, and a low score to ambient noise from various sources.
摘要：众所周知，人类言语和某些动物的声音可以传达有意义的内容，因为我们可以破译给定话语所传达的内容。本文探讨了一种确定信号是否有意义的替代方法，该方法仅分析信号本身，并且独立于所传达的含义可能是什么。我们设计了一种方法，以一个波形作为输入，并输出一个指示其“有意义”程度的分数。我们对输入的连续部分进行聚集，以最小化总描述长度，然后将分配的集群标签的代码长度作为意义分数。我们根据几个基线对我们的方法进行了经验评估，并表明它是唯一一种对各种语言和各种说话者的人类言语给予高分的方法，对鸟类和虎鲸的动物叫声给予中等分，对来自各种来源的环境噪音给予低分。

[NLP-42] Handling Numeric Expressions in Automatic Speech Recognition

点击查看摘要

Abstract:This paper addresses the problem of correctly formatting numeric expressions in automatic speech recognition (ASR) transcripts. This is challenging since the expected transcript format depends on the context, e.g., 1945 (year) vs. 19:45 (timestamp). We compare cascaded and end-to-end approaches to recognize and format numeric expression, such as years, timestamps, currency amounts, and quantities. For the end-to-end approach we employed a data generation strategy using a large language model (LLM) together with a text to speech (TTS) model to generate adaptation data. The results on our test dataset show that while approaches based on LLMs perform well on recognizing formatted numeric expressions, adapted end-to-end models offer competitive performance with the advantage of lower latency and inference cost.
摘要：本文解决了自动语音识别（ASB）成绩单中正确格式化数字表达的问题。这具有挑战性，因为预期的文字记录格式取决于上下文，例如，1945年（年）与19：45（时间戳）。我们比较了级联和端到端方法来识别和格式化数字表达，例如年、时间戳、货币金额和数量。对于端到端方法，我们采用了使用大型语言模型（LLM）和文本到语音（TTC）模型的数据生成策略来生成适应数据。我们测试数据集的结果表明，虽然基于LLM的方法在识别格式化数字表达方面表现良好，但调整后的端到端模型提供了有竞争力的性能，具有较低的延迟和推理成本的优势。

Abstract:Large Language Model (LLM) based agents have garnered significant attention and are becoming increasingly popular. Furthermore, planning ability is a crucial component of an LLM-based agent, involving interaction with the environment and executing actions to complete a planning task, which generally entails achieving a desired goal from an initial state. This paper investigates enhancing the planning abilities of LLMs through instruction tuning, referred to as agent training. Recent studies have demonstrated that utilizing expert-level trajectory for instruction-tuning LLMs effectively enhances their planning capabilities. However, existing work primarily focuses on synthesizing trajectories from manually designed planning tasks and environments. The evaluation results derived from AgentBoard show that AgentGen greatly improves LLMs’ planning ability, e.g., the AgentGen instruction-tuned Llama-3 8B surpasses GPT-3.5 in overall performance. 点击查看摘要

Abstract:Rapid advances in the capabilities of large language models (LLMs) have raised widespread concerns regarding their potential for malicious use. Open-weight LLMs present unique challenges, as existing safeguards lack robustness to tampering attacks that modify model weights. [AI-5] A Policy-Gradient Approach to Solving Imperfect-Information Games with Iterate Convergence

链接: https://arxiv.org/abs/2408.00751
作者: Mingyang Liu,Gabriele Farina,Asuman Ozdaglar
关键词-EN: reinforcement learning toolbox, stochastic trajectory feedback, importance sampling corrections, single-agent reinforcement learning, learning toolbox

*备注:

点击查看摘要

Abstract:Policy gradient methods have become a staple of any single-agent reinforcement learning toolbox, due to their combination of desirable properties: iterate convergence, efficient use of stochastic trajectory feedback, and theoretically-sound avoidance of importance sampling corrections. In multi-agent imperfect-information settings (extensive-form games), however, it is still unknown whether the same desiderata can be guaranteed while retaining theoretical guarantees. Instead, sound methods for extensive-form games rely on approximating counterfactual values (as opposed to Q values), which are incompatible with policy gradient methodologies. In this paper, we investigate whether policy gradient can be safely used in two-player zero-sum imperfect-information extensive-form games (EFGs). We establish positive results, showing for the first time that a policy gradient method leads to provable best-iterate convergence to a regularized Nash equilibrium in self-play.

[AI-8] Improving Retrieval-Augmented Generation in Medicine with Iterative Follow-up Questions

Abstract:The emergent abilities of large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated great potential in solving medical questions. In addition, we characterize the scaling properties of i-MedRAG with different iterations of follow-up queries and different numbers of queries per iteration. Our case studies show that i-MedRAG can flexibly ask follow-up queries to form reasoning chains, providing an in-depth analysis of medical questions. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first-of-its-kind study on incorporating follow-up queries into medical RAG.
